"Okay, say a few less drunken words, company commander,

Drunken words, not drunken words! If you don't believe me, go and see, watching her being played with by that bastard..." He cried... The smile also disappeared from the female shopkeeper's face.

After a moment of silence, he stood up suddenly, took out a handful of money, and rushed out without saying anything. The female shopkeeper felt as if a stone had fallen on her heart.

"God, I never thought..." Before she could finish a sentence, Li Dakui stumbled in again, he walked to the table, pulled out the sharp knife, and left the small hotel. (The End)

A Lesson in Life 206

— Family Member

In winter, the afternoon sun always hid in the layers of dark clouds. The office of the agency, with several bright electric lights turned on, was occupied by more than ten people, but it was quiet. Everyone lowered their heads and used pens to write or copy, which made the sound of the pen tips scratching on the paper even clearer. The red fire tongues of the stove lying at the base of the wall crackled from time to time, always breaking the silent atmosphere.

A clerk with a square face, a mouth and eyes that showed an annoying, calculating type, lifted the thick cloth door curtain and came in. With the sound of his footsteps, a gust of cold wind blew in, which caused eighteen pairs of eyes to instinctively focus on him, glance at him with dissatisfaction, and then shrink back. The clerk didn't care and walked to the desk of the accountant surnamed Li in the corner and threw a large red envelope on the table with an arrogant expression. Afterwards, he stood holding his short beard with his hand on his chin.

"What's the matter?" The accountant surnamed Li stopped writing and asked with a smile.

"You'll know when you read it yourself, official business." The clerk showed a contemptuous and impatient expression, as if he was very reluctant to talk to the other party, although he was one level lower than the accountant surnamed Li in terms of status, but his arrogant attitude at the moment was also not common. This made the accountant surnamed Li even more surprised.

"Official business?" The accountant surnamed Ji hesitated and glanced at the clerk before hesitantly grabbing the letter, tearing it open, and reading it. Suddenly his expression tightened, as if a criminal was reading a death sentence, so desperate and pale.

"It's an official letter of dismissal!" In addition to himself, two other colleagues were also dismissed. His fingertips trembled. He stared at it blankly, but he still couldn't believe it, and subconsciously read the letter silently again. There was no mistake, Li Haoran - his name, the three words flashed dazzlingly in his eyes, and instantly became three hammers that directly hit his head, more like a terrible muzzle, a ferocious demon, scaring away his courage and tearing apart all his hopes. Everything in front of him was completely dark, and he almost fainted.

"What's wrong, have you seen enough? Others still want to see it," the clerk deliberately raised his voice, which made him try his best to calm his confused mind.

Page 18

"Despicable!" The accountant surnamed Li watched the clerk's back as he walked away, gritting his teeth and cursing in his heart. "A job with a salary of thirty yuan a month was smashed for no reason," then he sighed softly for a while.

From this moment on, he was disconnected from everything here. He angrily dropped the pen that he had been using non-stop for ten hours a day for three months and wanted to stand up and walk out immediately. Yes, he was not qualified and was not allowed to stay in this room for another minute or even a second. Staying another minute or a second would make him feel more humiliated and embarrassed. Although in fact no one would immediately interfere with or drive him away, he felt that he needed to leave immediately anyway. But somehow, his legs suddenly cramped, and he simply lost the strength to walk a few steps. His buttocks seemed to be tightly glued to the chair by a sticky substance, and he couldn't break free.

What he was more keenly aware of was that a dozen colleagues seemed to understand the unfortunate and drastic change in his destiny that he had suffered in this short period of time, and as a result, there were a dozen gloating faces, and more than twenty faces that suddenly became very gloomy, with cold eyes, like arrowheads, all shooting at his whole body, piercing through his heart and piercing through his chest. He almost didn't have the courage to look up and look at the colleagues around him, no, now they were the faces of opposing enemies.

"Humans are cruel and have no sympathy" he cursed secretly in his heart again.

The office was still quiet, only he was listening to the sound of his mental balance slowly collapsing.

It was completely dark outside the window. Because there was a stove in the room, the temperature was very high and it was not cold. However, he was always trembling all over, and the blood in every blood vessel seemed to be freezing invisibly like ice.

Five o'clock struck. The colleagues all dispersed, and the room was empty, leaving only him alone. The handyman began to sweep the floor and tidy up the messy things on the table. He himself couldn't remember how he walked upstairs to the bedroom.

His mood was even darker in the night.

"Old Li, you don't have to be so depressed, what is a job of thirty yuan?"

A colleague who lived with him said in a comforting manner. Old Li only looked pale and stared blankly at the dim electric light for a long time without opening his mouth. Other people's words, no matter how good or enthusiastic they were, seemed to him now to be intentional sarcasm and ridicule.

"I've already lost my job, so what's the use of even if it's true sympathy?" he thought.

The clerk with a square face came in and said to him in a commanding tone:

"Hey, the director just said that it's best if you move out today, because someone will be moving in tomorrow." The title of Mr. Li was canceled.

"Is it impossible to move tomorrow? Uh, what will happen if I don't move today?" He was really angry. He said with great courage.

"It's always better to be proactive. It's boring to wait until people come and nag."

The clerk didn't face him, but walked out while talking.

He sighed heavily, and there were two puddles of clear water in the corners of his eyes, wandering and about to drip on his cheeks.

Good Flower Grove 207

— Mi Shan

Not far from our residence is a forest. All those who have traveled by boat on the Verdant Willow River and passed by our place know about this forest of ours. When those travelers stand on the bow of the boat, gazing idly around, they often exclaim in surprise, especially in the spring, when the forest becomes a cluster of flowers. The travelers shout even louder, "Beautiful flowers, beautiful flowers!" If it weren't for the river separating them, they would want to rush over there. – Once, someone almost fell into the water.

Most of these trees are fruit trees. Peach blossoms bloom in March, apricot blossoms in April, and pear blossoms in May. Throughout the spring, the air is filled with the fragrance of flowers. Therefore, many people traveling from Shandong to the northwest—they always go to the northwest in groups when the spring famine comes—must pass through here. Everyone doesn't have a name for this forest; they only sigh at the beauty of the flowers here, so they call this forest "Good Flower Grove."

Good Flower Grove is a great temptation to travelers – many people want to stay here and live. In the past, many more stayed behind. Some of them were very good at managing trees, making the flowers even more beautiful and the fruits even more delicious. Every year, boats loaded with fruits go downstream to exchange for unseen treasures. Besides fishing, Good Flower Grove gives us unlimited help in our lives.

It's not just materially; our lives in the spring were once as brilliant as flowers. Those young men and women like me all seemed intoxicated by the fragrance of spring flowers. When the moonlight covered the earth and the stars twinkled with happy eyes in the night, they would embrace and kiss each other like crazy, singing. They were all young people with boiling blood in their hearts, filling their veins, forgetting the pain that life had given them in their joy. No, there was no pain at that time. One of our female ancestors once said: "Love is like wine. Whether male or female, drinking it is beneficial. It can make people excited, hardworking, and brave. But, being drunk in the well of wine? You will be drowned." We young people believed in this saying.

However, the Verdant Willow River is a devil-like madman. It roars or swells its belly, making the vast wilderness all its territory. The houses we built with our blood and sweat, and our brothers-like, friendly cattle, sheep... were all swept away by its yellow mud wings.

This Good Flower Grove was also swept away by them.

It was a spring, when the peach blossoms were blooming scarlet red. Many young people happily called to their partners, "The peach blossoms are as red as your cheeks!" However, the river burst, and the endless water floated away all of us, and naturally the peach blossoms too!

We escaped the famine by boat, enduring all kinds of hardships. After the river returned to its course, we came back, rebuilt our simple houses, and continued our days. However, we no longer had that lovely grove of trees. Based on our experience, it would take four years to restore a small forest.

The disappearance of this forest seems to symbolize our lives: We no longer have brilliant days. Not only the old people are sighing in grief, but also the young people are like this—they have lost the sustenance of their springtime love.

We still think those travelers are better off than us. But, they told us, "The Northwest is not good either, understand? – Not to mention anything else, even children can't be sold!" Smoking a thick pipe, they seemed about to cry...

Some people began to plant trees, preparing to restore the spectacular appearance of the past – that brilliant spring, the symbol of spring. However, some people often sang a little song, saying, "Good Flower Grove is a place of happiness, restoring it is too difficult!" (Story of the Verdant Willow River, Part Three)

Storytelling with Stringed Instruments 209

He Yunfang, He Qinfang - Double Pearl Phoenix

Central-Western (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening "Eyes Cut Off the Wild Goose"

The beautiful woman looks at the hibiscus flower in the mirror. Parting from her talented lover causes great heartache. When he left, he promised to meet again when the willows are green and the peach trees are red. What talk of the Dragon Boat Festival, celebrating with red pomegranates? Spring goes, spring comes, and autumn arrives again. The Cowherd and Weaver Girl joyfully meet. Pushing open the window to view the bright autumn moon, Chang'e tightly closes the Guanghan Palace. Autumn passes, and winter arrives early. Cold winds blow in gusts. The lonely woman fears the end of winter. The hateful wronged soul, in such cold weather, may not necessarily suffer loneliness. They must meet someone who understands their feelings. If he doesn't come in this lifetime, so be it. Cut off all contact and send a letter. So that I don't worry about him all the time.

Xu Wenbi's Opening

Navigation (1180) 11:15 AM to 12:00 PM

Opening "Romance of the Western Chamber"

A scholar's feelings are worth half a piece of paper. One tael of silver provides for the meditation hall. He most delights in the blessed land of the Three Treasures. Meditating and listening to the Diamond Sutra. The cuckoo sings lonely by the ear. A traveler in a foreign inn feels even more desolate. Here is where the clear breeze and bright moon are unattended. Rest and sojourn in the Western Chamber. Sitting idly in a small pavilion, contemplating the principles of Yi. Opening a book by the firefly window, reciting essays. A pair of monks and laymen converse intimately. A maid walks out, dressed in green. To obey the command of Mistress Cui, she specifically sets up a ritual ground in the meditation room. To commemorate the death of the late Chancellor, she invites monks to pray for his ascent to the Western Paradise. On the fifteenth auspicious day, they worship the Dharma King. After speaking, she pauses, because she is a romantic fool who delivers rouge. Zhang Sheng comes forward and bows deeply. Elder sister, could you be Red Maid, the maid of Miss Yingying? I am Zhang Junrui, a talented scholar from Luoyang. I am using the monastery as a study for marriage reasons. Please report to the Palace of Pistil. Tell them I don't have a wife at home yet. Red Maid listens, her face changes. Sir, your words are too absurd. It is said from ancient times that one should not speak improperly. A reading gentleman is too frivolous. The old mistress is as unyielding as frost. No child over three feet is allowed into the main hall. What a maid hears can be forgiven. If the mistress finds out, she will be very angry. From now on, think before you speak.

Lingering Sounds

Since the Yaxingshe Mouth Opera Society recruited the first batch of free students, the number of new members has exceeded three times the original quota. Many who joined later still feel regretful. Therefore, in order to promote it, the association continued to recruit the second batch of new members. It is reported that the classes will officially start on the nineteenth of this month (Sunday). There are still some places left. To register and request a badge, please do so quickly. The address is No. 302, Nan Shi Road, Nanjing Road, inside the China Morning and Evening School.

Every Saturday at 4:00 PM, Mr. Zhang Yizhang, a cartoonist, hosts a cartoon lecture on Central-Western Radio. The topic for this period is "The Application of Perspective in Cartoons." Questions about cartoons can be sent to the address. (Sweetie)

The Mimi Collection magazine, published by the Yuanchang Advertising Company Broadcasting Station at No. 7, Sanrang Lane, Caishi Road, Shanghai, has released its first issue of Volume Three. This issue is a special comic issue, with more content. Each issue is sold for 30 cents. Advance subscriptions for the whole year are $1.21 including postage for local areas, and $2.32 including postage for out-of-town areas.

Movies

Color Film "Revenge at Pine Ridge" Starring Shirley Vernet Set to Premiere 213

"The Trail of the Lonesome Pine," a Paramount production and the first full-color outdoor film in screen history, will soon be screened in Shanghai. The film stars Shirley Vernet, Fred McMurray, and Henry Fonda; the director is specialist Hardie Hatcheway, who directed "Battleground" and other films. This film is entirely natural color and natural background, opening up a new era in film art. The story depicts the combative life of the residents of the Blue Ridge Mountains of America, and interspersed with a sad and beautiful story of three love affairs. The plot is tortuous and the performance is profound. It is not only superior in beautiful pictures. Paramount believes that it is one of the best works of this year, which is definitely not without reason. It is expected that it will cause a sensation again after three days of premiere.

Boris Karloff Starring in Horror Film "Revenge of the Walking Dead" 214

Premiering at the Great Light Theater on Saturday

Boris Karloff, who appeared on the screen in a terrifying posture, gained great fame after the release of the film "Frankenstein." Warner Pictures has recently hired him to star in the film "The Walking Dead," which is said to premiere at the Great Light Theater on Saturday. The film is based on the recent highly successful experiment in the scientific community. The plot extends the scientists' Nobel Prize winners, Carrel, and the world-admired Cornish's experiment of resuscitating newly dead animals. The scientific principle is the warp, and a bizarre revenge case is the weft. The interest is rich, the theme is novel, and the horror scenes in the film are even more than in "Frankenstein" and other films.

Shirley Temple's New Work "Little Pearl" 215

Premiering at the Tiantian Theater Tomorrow

Gu Lanjun Speaks 216

"Peaches and Plums Competing for Beauty" has already been shown at the Jincheng Grand Theater. Gu Lanjun's acting skills, who plays the sassy and bold Jasmine, have won applause and praise from every audience member. Yes, Gu Lanjun succeeded in "Peaches and Plums Competing for Beauty." Regarding this performance of "Peaches and Plums Competing for Beauty," Gu Lanjun stated the following opinions, she said:

"In the past, I have never taken on a role like the one that Mr. Li Pingqian asked me to take on. It always made me very worried. As for how good the results are now, I dare not say, but in good conscience, I have already fulfilled my due responsibility in acting skills. Of course, there are still unsatisfactory places, and of course, I hope that there will be progress in future works.

"Many people praise us for our good results. I only take it as an encouragement to me. I am determined to expect continued and greater efforts!"

That's right! We not only want to congratulate Miss Gu Lanjun on this amazing achievement, but we are also looking forward to Miss Gu's great efforts in the future. At the same time, we would like to recommend this "Peaches and Plums Competing for Beauty" to our readers. "Peaches and Plums Competing for Beauty" is currently being performed at the Jincheng Grand Theater.
